Aman, Anlan, and Anlu can be said to have the same origin (the founder of Aman holds shares in Anlan and Anlu for his entrepreneurial projects). Aman and Anlu are relatively similar. They are both types of ancient houses. Compared with the two , I prefer the modern comfort of Anlan.
There is Anadi in Shanghai that is equally comfortable. I have been there many times, but its overall value for money is higher in Xinchang Anlan.
Moreover, when comparing the reviews of several other Anlan brands, Xinchang Anlan is even better.
The following is my experience of staying at Xinchang Anlan:
-The geographical environment is unique. Here, there are mountains and water, the sunrise, sunset, starry sky are beautiful, and the air is fresh.
-The room is very high, and I like the temple-like emptiness. The pillows and quilts are down, making it easy to sleep. During the bath, the staff of the SPS depar**ent helped with disinfection and placement of Chinese medicine bath bags. Compared with the big bags of Chinese medicine that other hotels are so pretentious about, this small bag is unexpectedly easy to use. The Philips hair dryer that has been complained about looks cheap but actually feels good in use. Although it is naturally not as good as Dyson, it is also easier to use than the ordinary Panasonic. The only flaw is that the quality of the trouser clips is so poor that my fingers were accidentally scratched.
-The service is very good. I like our butler [Fu Jie] by name here. He is super considerate and thoughtful, and responds promptly. He is a young man and has smooth communication.
-Good food, rich breakfast, chefs prepare a lot on site, and there are many service staff. My favorite is the big taro, super delicious. The tofu pudding is also super delicious. However, the pastries are a bit sweet, so for now, Anadi is the number one hotel for food. But there is a "Xinchang Local Food Restaurant" nearby that is very delicious. I ate it twice in a row. Fat friends who see this post can try it. The ingredients are fresh and the recipes are delicious.
-Additional benefits and others: You can stay and play in the sports hall, which has billiards, table tennis and table football; the cocktails in the "swimming bar" are quite good. I drank a whiskey-based Longjing wine, which is quite special. I think this is better than many professional bars; travel photography privileges, free follow-up photos if you want, you have to pay 598 yuan; before leaving, the lady at the front desk gave two boxes of snacks, including coffee, water and bread, which was very considerate , I just don‚Äôt feel sleepy anymore while driving, thank you.
This should be almost the end of our experience. Finally, we would like to thank our butler [Fu Jie] for liking us again. We will probably go to Xinchang Anlan again.
